at Nimbal informing me, “Kamal is not now-a-days sing-
ing the song as Well as she used to sing formerly. Please
ask her to sing it with attention and devotion.”

21.   My eldest son Dr. Vishvanath,    M.R.C.P. who      is    at
present the Chief, Medical Services, California was ill at
Jaipur on account of Typhoid in 1953. Dr. G. D. Parikh,
Civil Surgeon, was attending on him.    Inspite of our great
care, the fever relapsed and we had to wait for forty-two
days,    Every alternate day,   I was writing to Professor
Ranade every detail     about   Vishvanath’s    condition.    On
the 4151 day, at night he had high fever, and as he began
to utter some words in delirium, I heard him speak three
or four times the words, “J am here, do not fear.” In the
morning at about 6.30   when the temperature came down
to 102, I asked him if he had a dream.        He told me that
he was being taken      on stretcher   from    one    room     to
another in the S.M.S. Hospital, Jaipur.        In   every room
1 saw Prof, Ranade sitting and he was saying to me, “I am

here, do not fear.” The same morning at about 8, the
temperature Came to normal and after the next three or
four days it used to remain normal throughout day and
night,   My wife and I were surpised to know that the
Saving power of the Guru can penetrate not only the three
States of life, namely, the waking, the sleeping and the
dreaming, but also the delirium in high fever.


22:   Twice successively in 1967 and 1968 I was saved, I
believe by the grace of God. First while driving away a
pigeon, I happened to fall flat on the corner of my cot.
It hit hard the left ribs and I screamed so loudly and
painfully that my wife rushed out of the bathroom to
276 = Prof. R. 9. Ranade and His Spiritual Lineage


see what had happened.           I could neither breathe well nor
Speak a word      With her.      With great difficulty      I got into
a tonga which my neighbour late Mr. Bhaludada brought
for    mé     ahd I was    taken     to    a    neighbouring      doctor,
Mr, Chatierji by name who had an X-ray plant. I request-
ed the doctor to have an           x-ray       photograph   but       after
examining me thoroughly he told me that I should thank
God in that my left lung was not ruptured and that I
narrowly escaped death.          As there       was no necessity        of
X-ray photograph, he merely told me to apply an adhesive
tape for about ten days           and     do    nothing   else.   I    did
accordingly and I was cured.



      More serious than this was the severe stomach-ache
from which I suffered for about a fort-night. Dr. K.
Banerji gave me several medicines, but ‘as I took them
the pain became all the more unbearable.              The liver was
enlarged and there was constant and severe pain not only
on the liver but all through the ribs on the                right     side
right upto the chest.       Normal breathing too became for
me a great exercise. On one Tuesday evening I went out
for a short walk of a furlong or 50, because there was
Prof, Mohanlal Sharma to accompany me.                    With      great
difficulty,   I could   finish    that    walking    race    with      my
friend, with my right hand on my liver, and the left ०7
the back side of my right ribs.           As the medicines did not
help and as the pain persisted, I plainly told               my       wife
that I would not touch any medicine and that I had given
myself entirely into the hands of God.               “Let   Him now
save me or kill me,” said I in despair. We went to bed,
but within an hour or so, a severe wave of pain woke
me up, There were tears in my eyes afd I prayed most
ardently to God to save me. I did not wak2 up my wife
for there was 10 sense in making her miserable along
with me.      I looked into the photo of Ranade, Baba and
Bhausahib and said to God, “I know you can cure me
without medicine, henceforth I shall not take any medicine.
Why are you leaving me to my fate? Save me by the
                                  Appendix                           शा


power of your grace.”             JI repeated my prayer again             and
again and within a few minutes I slept soundly only to
get up at about 6.30 in the morning. There was absolutely
no pain but the ghost of doubt and fear was there. I told
my wife to alow me not to have the medicine for a day
or two.     That day on Dr. Banerji’s instruction, Mr. M. P.
Vyas, had sent a compounder to test my blood. I request-
ed the gentleman to come after two days during which
time also, there was not the slightest of pain. One week
passed, two weeks passed and I had no pain.                        I told the
story to my friend Mr. M. P. Vyas Atuji as he is called.
Possibly he must have told the same to Dr. Banerji whom
I was trying to avoid.            He felt glad at my recovery and
said, ‘God is great.’        I    began to have an evening stroll
every     day,    After   about      three or   four        weeks     I   met
Dr. Banerji just outside the hospital.             He         congratulated
me and feeling my liver by his hand said that there was
no enlargement at all.             Since that day till now that is
during the last thirteen years, I am free from pain in my
stomach,        Should I not believe in the kindness and,
                                                          grace
of God ? I do not think,
                      it necessary to prove it to others.
T only know that my Guru is great.

23.   My son-in-law, Mr. Moreshwarpant Soman had                          just
recovered from typhoid, but soon afterwards at Indore he

again suffered from severe stomach-ache and fever. ‘One
day, in the year 1971 being unable to bear any longer,
he prayed to Shri Gurudeva Ranade whose photo was
kept in front of his bed and said, “How long am I to suffer
like this? Be Kind unto me.” Soon he went into a sort
of Slumber,       when    he      heard   a voice coming           from   the
direction   of the     photograph,        “Apply   the      holy    angara.”
Forthwith he called my daughter and taking the angara,
She applied it to his body. Within a short time the tem-
perature came to normal and the pain                   in     the stomach
stopped,    >


24.   In the year 1973, Raghunath, my second son got a
covetable       job on Rs,       3,000/- per month       in    the    Petro-
278   87. R. D. Ranade and His Spiritual Lineage

chemical    Works,    an   Indian     Government     concern    at
Baroda.    He sold every small or great thing that belong-
ed to him including a fine house of his own in New Jersey.
But after he worked for some time in Baroda, he got so
much sick of the affairs there that he wrote to mé that
he intended to go back to the U.S.A. With great difficulty
he stayed in Baroda with his wife and three gong in order
to satisfy me only,    “I do not want cheap        money,    I do
not wish to be idle and yet draw my salary. ‘I do not
find that the work I do is my work in which I take interest
and joy neither can I flatter anyone        nor do I wish      ४०
be flattered,” so wrote my son to mé.         I then permitted
him to return to the States,        Forthwith in the year 1974
‘he returned after suffering a net loss of two 1908 of rupees.
With courage and a strong will he went back and with
the grace of God is in a far better position at Trumbull
and is getting much more as a Head          of the   big   plastic
company than what-he was getting at Baroda.            After his
return to the States, my wife was greatly anxious about
him, One day she saw Ranade in her dream.            He inquired
about everyone of us. She said to him that she was then
only anxious aboyt Raghunath.          Seeing her gloomy and
sobbing, Ranade told her that Raghunath had got a good job,
so she should not be anxious about him. Eight days later
we got a letter from Raghunath saying that he was well
and had got a fine job.



25. It was on Sunday the 28th of April, 1974 that my
wife, Malatibai bécame suddently véry ill. The Sunday
meditational programme was just
                              to start when she began
to cough and vomit a lof. She became immediately so
weak that she had to be helped in order to reach the bed.
One could hardly stand at a distance of six to eight feet
for the vomit of her cough wag smélling foul. She was
given Homeopathic médicine for a few days. Afterwards
Dr. K. Banerji examined her, Even her first X-ray plate
showed that her left lung was greatly affected. Dr. Banerji
was doing his best and yet as days passed on the X-ray
                          Appendix                               279


showed more and more deterioration in her condition Dr.
S. K. Pande the surgeon was then consulted. The team of
doctors thought that Bronchoscopy should first-be tried at
Bikaner. My wife did not take any objection to anything
being done to her, It was a miracle that when all prepa-
ration was made for her being carried to           Bikaner,      the
plan was suddenly dropped.        No body knew          what     she
told after her full recovery that Ranade appeared in her
dreams and visions and moved his hand over her body.
One thing,   we   the   attendants.   Dr. Isvarachand Metted
Anand Kumar Vyas and myself could observe from out-
side was that Malatibai was found to be meditating on
the Name of God day and might and was not concerned
about her high fever or the worsening condition of her
body, The last X-ray that was taken on the Ist of June
showed a sudden and remarkable progress which made
the   doctors too exclaim     with    surprise.   “A    miraculous
recovery.”   Dr. Pande who came to our house that even-
ing said, “I never thought she would recover so suddenly.”
That day I sent a telegram to my son Dr. Vishvanath in
US.A, “Thank God fifty percent improvement wife out
of danger as doctors think.”      Indeed blessed is       he    who
sees the hand of God.      Afterwards, one day in course of
conversation I said to a renowned doctor, “Will it not be

more correct to say, “He treats and He cures,          than saying
व treat and He cures?” “Yes, certainly,” he replied. But
1 said to myself,   a miracle may not occur unless one is -
first tested by God, but who would pass the test of God,
unless God showers ‘His grace upon him ?

26. On the 15th of February, 1975, I became suddenly
ill at Jodhpur,   At about 4.30 in the evening I began to
vomit the tarry, black     coloured   bile mixed       with    blood.

Dr. 8, K. Pande soon removed me to the Government
Hospital. There my condition worsened, pulse became
bad, I could not speak a word, hands and feet began to
be colder and colder. There was no other alternative for
the surgeon Dr. Pande but to use his knife as the last
temedy to save my life.     But a few friends of mine chiefly
280     Prof. R. 2. Ranade and His Spiritual Lineage


Mr, Shivashanker Joshi with        tears       in his    eyés touched
Dr, Pande’s feet and implored him net to operate on my
stomach,     probably    because       he    remembered        Professor
Ranade’s advice to me not to allow any operation. Twice
again I vomitted large quantities of blood, and I hung my
head     backwards,     saying   the        words,    ‘O God, O God’.
Everything was finished was the common thought of all
but as they say all were         surprised       to   see   me      living.
Within a few seconds at the most I brought                     my    head
forward.    The saline and the blood            drippings      and     the
injections and    oral medicines found their            way and the
very kind    services of doctors, compounders and                friends
were so Overwhelming that it took only six days for me
to enable Dr. Pande to discharge me from the hospital.
Once again in the opinion of the doctors, there occurred
a miracle which was beyond the                scope   of the     medical
science,




27.    On the top of all these miracles, there is the greatest
living Miracle that the uniqué devotional Ganga which
has taken its rise at Siddhagiri near Kolhapur, in Maha-
yashtra and has passed through the disirict of Bijapur in
Karnataka, has found its way in the deserts of Rajasthan.
A host of seekers, not less than 200, went to Nimbal and
got themselves initiated at the Samadhi of Shri Gurudeva
Ranade. Every one of them, rich or poor, must have spent
Rs. 300/- or Rs. 350/- for travelling and other expenses
voluntarily, Excepting eight or teh who 18५6 been thrown
out of the stream of devotion on account of their own
folly ‘of ingratitude and arrogance, all have moré or less
reaped the harvest of the moral and spiritual life and are
not left behind in material prosperity also; One has only
to cone to Jodhpur and seé for himself if what I have
written ig true or not, Let him meet any one of those
who liavé become established in their devotion to Gurt
and to God and eonte to any conclusion he likes.
                          Appendix                            281


     There are some other genuine miracles which I know,
but they have not occurred in connection           with   anyone
connected with my family.      They are as below:


1,   Mr.     Dadasahib    Deshpande’s    mother-in-law        and
Babasahib Sangoram’s wife had halted at Allahabad on
her return journey from Benaras to Athani, Professor
Ranade 100 her to stay for a few days more, but she left
the place.   As she was a diabetic patient she was brought
to Sangli, and she was to be operated upon her toe of the
foot.    Dadasahib went to Sangli with      the blessings and
angara of Gurudeva.      Soon after   in the vacation Ranade
too On his way to Nimbal casually stopped at Sangli and
went to see the condition of Mrs, Sangorama. He got the
bandage opened by her and then looked into the wound.
Next day, when she went to the hospital the surgeon said,
“There is remarkable change for the better, I think there
is no need of an operation.” Mrs. Sangorama was cured
without any operation,



2.   Dr. ह. H. Karmarkar is a         well-known    surgeon    in
Bombay, His father who was himself a doctor at Modhol
was suffering from dropsy.     He came over to Nimbal with
the determination either to die at his Guru’s feet or to be

Saved by his grace, He used to tell others that he had
Stopped all medicines and was cured at Nimbal by eating
only the bread with the butter-milk which of course was
no medicine for dropsy.     The real medicine was the grace
of Prof, Ranade,

3.   Mr, Nanasahib Haridasa was suffering from T. 8.
glands.    On being advised by Professor Ranade he con-
Sulted     Dr. 8. प्र. Karmarkar, the famous surgeon of
Dadar Bombay, who told him that he should immediately
undergo an operation,   Mr. Haridasa returned to Nimbal
and insisited upon his accompanying Ranade to Allahabad.
After going over there Mr. Haridasa found that Ranade
Was Occupied with his various duties 2nd that therefore
282   Prof. R. D. Ranade and His Spiritual Lineage

he Could not inquire about the    condition   of   the TB.
glands.   After about three weeks all of a sudden Ranade
asked Mr, Haridasa “What about your glands? Are they
giving you trouble as before ?” Haridasa untied the piece
of cloth which he had tied round his neck and said. “They
have grown, I think, bigger than what they were before.”
On seeing them Ranade Said, “That is very good, there is
decidedly an improvement. Carry on your meditation
and apply a little water to them after every half an hour
of your meditation.”   Haridasa did as he was instructed
and after about a week or so, the glands burst open, and
Haridasa became free from the horrible disease. “Now go
to Dr. Karmarkar, and let him say whether you are really
free from the disease or not,” said Professor Ranade to
Haridasa, Waridasa did accordingly and what the doctor
said was “This is a cure which is beyond the province
of medicine or surgery.”
